I trick to filling up piping bags is if you get a jug, put the bag in the jug and gold the edges of the bag over the edge of the jug. That way it keeps the bag solid and open. You also pipe it from the bottom of the mixture.

ok more churro stuff that I've even tried IT WORKS I couldn't find a website that was good so I will tell the directions  make normal churro mix and put it into an icing bag ( don't freeze the icing bag) get a muffin tin turn it upside down and swirl the churro mix around and cover the top quickly, they fall apart. then freeze for an hour  when an hour is up take them out use a knife to peel them off one at a time,  put them in the oil one at a time when you take one off put the rest in the freezer when done roll them in cinnamon and sugar then put ice cream in them I've tried it it works really well

Straight guys should't attempt to make -baked- fried goods...  First you fold the pastry bag in half to avoid messes when filling it up. Second you make sure the batter goes all the way to the tip of the bag and the back side is closed/tied/folded before you squeeze it out. Third you need to know the CORRECT TEMPERATURE and keep it stable while you do anything with flower, or in other words your oil was too hot.

Hahaha this was great! Although... note to Rob... You made what is called a choux pastry, which is what's used for making churros... So you did that right! Good work! But as you noticed... one of the main ingredients in a choux (pronounced "shoe) pastry, is BUTTER. When butter gets cold, it gets hard. So don't let it cool down so much next time :) Other than that, good work man!
